          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Figensoft builds state of the art messaging solutions and payment systems. Messaging solutions include bulk SMS, MMS, email, and two-way messaging. Payment solutions include QR payments, virtual POS, and soft POS. 

Our global SMS hub solution enables multi national companies to deliver SMS worldwide. Development APIs are SMPP, Web service, XML, HTTP, Json, Java, COM API. We have solutions that satisfy more than 15.000 clients worldwide. Group companies are located in Azerbaijan, Georgia, and Turkish Republic of North Cyprus. 

Payment systems enable enterprises collect money easily and securely. QR payment solution is a safe contactless payment solution that has benefits for both merchants and cardholders.

Group companies have licenses for telecommunications and payments wherever applicable.
